# WWDC 2018 Keynote

## Summary
WWDC 2018 Keynote

## Info
* Featured
* WWDC 2018 - Session 101 - iOS, macOS, tvOS, watchOS
* https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/

ARKit.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1326) [ARKit opens up the world of AR](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1329) [to hundreds of millions of](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1331) [users, making it the world's](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1333) [largest AR platform by far.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1335) [And we're on a relentless pace](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1338) [of advancement with AR, and that](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1340) [continues today with ARKit 2.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1342) [Yes. ARKit 2 delivers advances](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1346) [with improved face tracking,](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1351) [more realistic rendering, and](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1353) [support for 3D object detection](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1355) [and persistence, which enables](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1358) [launching into AR experiences](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1359) [associated with a particular](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1362) [object or a physical space, like](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1363) [starting a game built around a](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1366) [physical toy or having a](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1367) [physical classroom serve as the](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1369) [foundation for a lesson that was](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1370) [authored in AR.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=1372) [But probably how it works.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6828) [Just like you can be identified](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6829) [by a fingerprint, it turns out](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6831) [that when you browse the web,](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6833) its](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6839) [like its configuration, its](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6839) you](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6844) [might have on the device.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6845) [And these data companies can use](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6846) [the set of characteristics to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6848) [construct a unique fingerprint](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6850) [to track your device from site](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6852) [to [much harder for trackers to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6857) [create a unique fingerprint.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6860) [We're presenting webpages with](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6862) [only a simplified system](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6863) [configuration.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6864) [We show them only built-in](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6866) [fonts, and Legacy plug-insulin](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6867) [are no longer supported, so](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6870) [those can't contribute to a](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6871) [fingerprint, and as a result,](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6872) [your Mac will look more like](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6874) [everyone else's Mac, and it will](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6876) [be dramatically more difficult](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6878) [for data companies to uniquely](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=6879) [identify your device and And that's all rendered](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=7303) [live on a MacBook running with](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=7306) [an eGPU.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=7309) [It's pretty great.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=7310) [[ Applause ]](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=7311) [Now another [learning.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=7321) [And today ML specialists [Swift.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=7372) [In fact, you can use Xcode](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=7373) fast.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=7383) [Now, as an example, we worked](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=7386) the](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=7389) [camera to identify objects and](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=7390)
